{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2020-10-09 11:33:10","updatedTime":"2020-10-09 11:33:10","title":"This 360° tabletop studio promises to make professional product photography ridiculously easy","link":"https://www.yankodesign.com/?p=280588","description":"<p><iframe title=\"Foldio360 Smart Dome - Expand your creativity\" src=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/orangemonkie/foldio360-smart-dome/widget/video.html\" height=\"590.625\" width=\"1050\" frameborder=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\"></iframe></p>\n<p>As an initial backer of the original Foldio photo studio, it&#8217;s pretty amazing to see how far the product line has come in terms of evolution, going from a simple idea that championed portability, to a more expert solution that gives you pro-features. The original Foldio from 2013 (I&#8217;ve still got mine) was quite literally a foldable photo-studio that could fit in an envelope that slid under your door. 7 years later, the original Foldio is still a great product for hobbyists and amateur photographers, but is a different beast compared to the Foldio360 Smart Dome, which offers a stunning list of features that make it the most comprehensive photo-studio for product photography and animation-work. A little larger than a basketball, the Foldio360 Smart Dome is a smart-studio that creates the perfect environment for product photography. it allows you to mount the camera of your choice (a DSLR or a smartphone), and click stunning photos of your product with a seamless white background and zero sharp shadows. A mechanical turntable even lets you capture products from every angle or create rotating animations of it.</p>\n<p>The Foldio360 Smart Dome is for creators and for creatives. Whether you have your own Etsy store or online store, or you&#8217;re just a product photographer or animator by profession, the Foldio360 Smart Dome helps you take that quintessential white-background product shot. The studio&#8217;s spherical design helps reflect light efficiently, creating a seamless, shadow-less scene with a pristine white background and a clearly illuminated product. LED strips embedded into the side of the sphere come with adjustable brightness and temperature, allowing you to perfectly white-balance your photos as you shoot them. A snap-on hood on the front lets you further cut reflections to create a more neutral environment, and openings on the front, as well as the top of the Foldio360 Smart Dome, let you take photos from a variety of angles.</p>\n<p>Once you set the studio up, a clamp on the front (with its own spirit level) lets you attach your shooting device &#8211; a smartphone or a professional camera. The Foldio360 Smart Dome even comes with a mechanical turntable that you can place your product on, giving you the ability to capture it from 360° &#8211; a feature that&#8217;s great for online retail, 3D-scanning, or animation. All of Foldio360 Smart Dome&#8217;s aforementioned features find a home in the Foldio app, which allows you to control your studio all from a touchscreen interface. You can change the brightness/temperature of the LED lights, rotate the turntable, and even automate the photography process, allowing the Foldio360 Smart Dome to rotate on its own while your smartphone routinely takes pictures without you needing to do anything! Professional product photography couldn&#8217;t be any easier than that!</p>\n<p>Designer: Orangemonkie</p>\n<p><a href=\"http://bit.ly/Fd360dome\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><strong>Click Here to Buy Now: $320</strong></a> <del datetime=\"2020-10-08T08:46:34+00:00\">$399</del> ($79 off). It offers customizable lighting, no shadow concerns, and less photoshop editing.</p>\n<p><a href=\"http://bit.ly/Fd360dome\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-281088\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/10/this-360-tabletop-studio-promises-to-make-professional-product-photography-ridiculously-easy/Foldio360_all_in_one_smart_photo_studio_01.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"1050\" /></a></p>\n<p>Foldio360 brings photo quality to everyone. Because traditional photo studios are overpriced, time-consuming, and require professional training to use. The newly designed dual shell structure uniquely diffuses the light in the interior, eliminating light reflection in your photos. -991_19238f9c81aa1a56.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/yankodesign/~4/B9E-74xCprA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn2@2020_1/2020/10/09/03-33-26-199_5cf47467748b1b07.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1602214390153},{"createdTime":"2020-10-09 11:33:10","updatedTime":"2020-10-09 11:33:10","title":"This hubless e-bike for urban environment rides just as smooth as it looks!","link":"https://www.yankodesign.com/?p=280654","description":"<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-280655\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/10/auto-draft/01_OohBike_VictorTabares_ECityBike.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>Living in a big city without a car sometimes means compromise. A trip to the grocery store might take a measly five minutes by car, but it’s another story on foot. That’s why <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/tag/electric-bike/\">electric bikes</a> have risen in popularity amongst city dwellers. Practically at each intersection, whether you’re in Los Angeles or Paris, rows of charged-up city bikes wait patiently to hit the streets. It’s always tempting to unlock one, with the sun beating down as the walk to the grocery reaches almost an hour. It’s no wonder, Victor Tabares, a designer based in bustling Barcelona, felt inspired to design and produce OOH BIKE.</p>\n<p>Since this e-bike retains its pedaling capabilities, most of the standout features from OOH BIKE are integrated into the bicycle itself. Just within the cyclist’s periphery vision, the battery levels are displayed along the top of the bicycle’s frame. Lit-up, neon lights signify the bicycle’s battery levels by the quarter. The front wheel on the OOH BIKE is entirely hubless, producing a metropolitan finished look that gives an otherwise integrated and functional bike some style. Additionally, the spokeless front helps rotate the wheel quickly and with little effort. While centerless wheels are primarily, it seems, an aesthetic decision, they do work well in city environments.</p>\n<p>Centerless wheels promote torque, quickening the brake’s response time, so you can stealthily slink your way through your city’s traffic lights and cross-sections. Between the handlebars, a mini screen from <a href=\"https://www.brose-ebike.com/de-en/homepage/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Brose Drive</a>, an automotive supplier that develops sensor systems for electric bikes, displays menu options, speed, and other digital information that’s easily accessible during any ride. Whether you’re on the cobblestoned avenues of London or riding along the earthquake-ridden pavement of San Francisco, OOH BIKE’s adjustable seat and integrated cable system make it the ideal, sleek bike for any city dweller.</p>\n<p>Designer: <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/victorproductdesign\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Victor Tabares</a></p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone /Obkb2x20YD0":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn87@2020_5/2020/10/09/03-33-27-086_33e96acd72fd4958.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1602214390153},{"createdTime":"2020-10-09 11:33:10","updatedTime":"2020-10-09 11:33:10","title":"The Lexus Design Award is on a mission to make the world better. Only 3 days left to enter!","link":"https://www.yankodesign.com/?p=281069","description":"<p><iframe title=\"Call for Entries I Lexus Design Award 2021\" width=\"1050\" height=\"591\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/K8sZqVDVZwM?feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen></iframe></p>\n<p>I&#8217;ve noticed something rather interesting over the past couple of years. The purpose of a design, any design, is to see itself evolve in a way that benefits users as well as the designer that had the idea in the first place. A well-designed product isn&#8217;t something that can exist in isolation with a ribbon pinned to it&#8230; yet most award programs do just that. They look at products, identify a few of them which look promising, give them a certificate or trophy, and move on to the next product&#8230; and the process repeats itself year after year. Most award programs don&#8217;t incubate great ideas into wonderful products&#8230; they just identify them and put them on a website for others to see, and that&#8217;s something I&#8217;ve come to identify with a lot of awards, but not the Lexus Design Award.</p>\n<p>Imagine having great designers gather around your idea and nourish it into something truly fruitful. Imagine having all the resources you need to prototype your idea into something that WORKS&#8230; not on paper, in reality. Imagine spending 3 months under the wing of industry-leading mentors who help guide you through the design process. The Lexus Design Award isn&#8217;t really like other awards&#8230; it&#8217;s part award, part internship, part incubator, and part institute. When you apply for the Lexus Design Award, you&#8217;re enrolling yourself into a 3-month course with internationally-recognized mentors like Joe Doucet (Founder, Joe Doucet x Partners), Mariam Kamara (Principal Architect, Atelier Masomi), Sputniko! (Associate Professor of Design at the Tokyo University of the Arts), and Sabine Marcelis (Founder, Studio Sabine Marcelis. Out of all the award participants, 6 Finalists are chosen to be a part of this mentorship experience. During this time, the mentors work with you ON your project (sort of like the most personalized internship ever), taking your rough concept to fruition, while Lexus incubates the product with as much as 3 million Japanese Yen or $25,000 dedicated to prototyping the projects to a working proof-of-concept.</p>\n<p>The Lexus Design Award’s core objective has always been to foster great ideas and great talent. Creating the perfect environment for a design to grow, Lexus helps engineer ideas into real, impactful solutions for a better future. The awards are free for all, focusing on young talent looking to find their footing in the industry, and offering them the ability to take their nascent ideas to new heights, with advice from established professional mentors. At the end of the mentorship phase, a Grand Prix finalist is chosen by the award&#8217;s esteemed judging panel comprising of Paola Antonelli (Senior Curator at MoMA), Greg Lynn (Architect and CEO Piaggio Fast Forward), Dong Gong (Founder &#38; Design Principal of Vector Architects), and Simon Humphries (Head of Toyota and Lexus Global Design).</p>\n<p>Entries for the 2021 edition of the Lexus Design Award are now open, with the theme echoing Lexus&#8217; brand principle &#8211; &#8220;Anticipate, Innovate and Captivate for a better tomorrow&#8221;. Head to the Discover Lexus website to submit your own designs for a chance to collaborate with world-class mentors and incubate your ideas into reality, or scroll down to check out some of the past winners of the Lexus Design Award as inspiration!</p>\n<p><strong><a href=\"https://bit.ly/2GgOEq3\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Submit Your Designs Now</a></strong> for Lexus Design Award 2021. Last Date for Submissions: October 11th, 2020.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/2GgOEq3\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-281070\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/10/the-lexus-design-award-is-on-a-mission-to-make-the-world-better-only-3-days-left-to-enter/call_for_entries_for_Lexus_Design_Award_2021_layout.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></a></p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">Lexus Design Award Past Winners</h4>\n<p>Lexus first launched this annual international award in 2013 to nurture up-and-coming designers and help them realize their vision around the future of design.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/2GgOEq3\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"size-full wp-image-268429 alignnone\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/07/designing-for-a-better-tomorrow-the-innovative-spirit-that-drives-the-lexus-design-awards-2020/lda2020_grand_prix_5.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></a></p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">Open Source Communities by BellTower (2020 Grand Prix Winner)</h4>\n<p>A vast number of Kenyans suffer from a combination of problems like water shortage, diseases caused by consumption of unfiltered/unfit water, having to walk miles to get water on a daily basis, or alternatively having to pay high rates for local water distribution. “In Nairobi, high-tech coexists with urban poverty”, say the team at BellTower, who designed the Open Source Communities project which creates a new format of community-building that relies on efficient allocation of resources that help the lower-income communities get access to basic necessities like water. The project creates a centralized water-reservoir – a structure that sits between hundreds of homes, providing water to every single one of them. The structure’s innovative format allows it to harvest and conserve rainwater, while actively filtering it of dirt, microorganisms, and other impurities. During the monsoons, surplus water helps generate money for the communities too, allowing them to get an extra source of income while bridging the vast resource gap. However, the best part about the Open Source Communities is that it exists as a public-utility template. Its open-source nature gives it unlimited flexibility, allowing it to be modified to fit in practically any scenario.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/2GgOEq3\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"size-full wp-image-278331 alignnone\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/09/draft-lda-call-for-entries/lexusdesignaward_2020_past_winners_1.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></a></p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">Algorithmic Lace by Lisa Marks (2019 Grand Prix Winner)</h4>\n<p>Bringing Algorithms and Attire together in a beautifully crafted garment with a noble purpose, Algorithmic Lace uses advanced three-dimensional modeling to handcraft bespoke bras for breast cancer survivors who have undergone mastectomy surgery. Algorithms have a long-standing love-affair with the textile industry, as one of the first machines to use algorithms was the Jacquard Loom back in the 1800s. The loom was controlled by a series of punched cards, which contained information that the loom read. Different cards had different algorithms into it and by switching the cards in the loom, you could tell it to alternate between complex textile weaves like brocade, damask and matelassé. Algorithmic Lace builds on that rich history, by using lines of code to create bras that are custom-built for their wearers. These garments are made specifically to functionally suit women who&#8217;ve undergone surgery, and the algorithmic pattern helps create a well-fitted, comfortable brassiere that&#8217;s also incredibly aesthetic to look at, empowering the wearer with confidence, along with their new lease of life.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/2GgOEq3\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"size-full wp-image-278334 alignnone\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/09/draft-lda-call-for-entries/lexusdesignaward_2020_past_winners_3.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></a></p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">Pixel by Hiroto Yoshizoe (2017 Grand Prix Winner)</h4>\n<p>There&#8217;s sheer magic in how the Pixel can actually take what you see and reduce its resolution to a handful of pixels&#8230; creating an illusion of being in a low-res world. At its heart is a uniquely crafted module that takes light as an input, and through repeated internal reflection, turns inputted images into square outputs. Imagine how the mirrors on a periscope work, taking an image from the top and carrying them down to the viewfinder below&#8230; this module does something similar, but with a different result. Stack enough of these modules together and you get the Pixel, a dynamic wall that instantly pixelates anything behind it. The Pixel relies on a powerful light source, and in this case, uses a projector. Project an image on it and the modules average out the light entering them, instantly pixelating the image and giving us a new perspective on the way we see light and shadows!</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/2GgOEq3\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"size-full wp-image-278335 alignnone\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/09/draft-lda-call-for-entries/lexusdesignaward_2020_past_winners_4.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></a></p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">Agar Plasticity by AMAM (2016 Grand Prix Winner)</h4>\n<p>As its name suggests, the Agar Plasticity project uses Agar, a gelatinous marine algal material, as a replacement for plastics, creating a naturally occurring alternative to one of nature&#8217;s largest pollutants. Perfectly encapsulating the Lexus theme of &#8216;designing for a better tomorrow&#8217;, the project envisions a use of Agar as an alternative to the plastics found in packaging. Given that packaging for a product is often discarded immediately after purchase, Agar Plasticity hopes to create a solution that is eco-friendlier. Agar itself is derived from nature, and when treated a certain way, can be molded into containers, trays, and films that can replace single-use plastics. When discarded, the Agar can easily degrade in water or land, turning into nutrition for microorganisms and helping reduce waste. Japan-based design-trio AMAM is currently working to get larger institutions and corporations to look into the use of Agar as a safe plastic-alternative.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/2GgOEq3\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-278817\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/09/the-lexus-design-award-is-on-a-mission-to-make-the-world-better-heres-how-you-can-participate/lexusdesignaward_past_winners_1.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></a></p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">Inaho by Hideki Yoshimoto and Yoshinaka Ono (2013 Grand Prix Winner)</h4>\n<p>Yet another example of how lighting can be more of an experience, Inaho captures the tranquil beauty of watching rice-plants sway in the breeze. Created by Japanese duo Hideki Yoshimoto and Yoshinaka Ono, Inaho captures a strong Japanese cultural element, creating something that&#8217;s not just eye-catching but also rooted in history. The lights come mounted on tall, flexible metal rods, which gently lean towards people as they approach it. The interactive element doesn&#8217;t just make the Inaho interesting in a tactile sense, it also creates a wonderful series of moving highlights and shadows as the rice-plant-inspired lamps lean in your direction as you approach them, prompting you to move closer. The word Inaho literally translates to &#8216;a ear of rice&#8217; in Japanese.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/2GgOEq3\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-278816\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/09/the-lexus-design-award-is-on-a-mission-to-make-the-world-better-heres-how-you-can-participate/call_for_entries_for_Lexus_Design_Award_2021_2.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"188\" /></a></p>\n<p>Submissions are being accepted until October 11th, 2020.</p>\n<div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a 03-33-24-859_be70ddf18521ce99.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/yankodesign?i=OcNb7gHb5zA:NQaWNEa4AfY:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn13@2020_3/2020/10/09/03-33-26-418_98193dee7935984f.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/yankodesign?d=7Q72WNTAKBA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn59@2020_6/2020/10/09/03-33-21-727_a7bab000502b2c11.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/yankodesign?i=OcNb7gHb5zA:NQaWNEa4AfY:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn12@2020_2/2020/10/09/03-33-22-719_d3c1abc9bb7676d9.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/yankodesign?i=OcNb7gHb5zA:NQaWNEa4AfY:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn35@2020_5/2020/10/09/03-33-22-891_3400b2c9f76e5670.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/yankodesign?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn46@2020_5/2020/10/09/03-33-23-991_19238f9c81aa1a56.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/yankodesign/~4/OcNb7gHb5zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn31@2020_6/2020/10/09/03-33-26-611_ec43440cb50aa0f4.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1602214390152},{"createdTime":"2020-10-09 11:33:10","updatedTime":"2020-10-09 11:33:10","title":"Aston Martin’s V12 roofless speedster is a sleek siren calling out to all thrill seekers!","link":"https://www.yankodesign.com/?p=281024","description":"<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-281036\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/10/aston-martin-v12-roofless-speedster-reminds-us-all-that-the-road-is-calling/Aston-Martin-V12-roofless-speedster_Roadster_3.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>Post cancellation of the Geneva International Motor Show 2020, the <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/tag/aston-martin/\">Aston Martin</a> V12 showed its gorgeous face at the company’s headquarters in Gaydon, Warwickshire in March. The lightweight two-seater speedster is designed by the “Q by Aston Martin” bespoke division, who took the car from the blueprint stage to reality in just 12 months. Now the car inspired by the CC100 Speedster Concept and 1959 Le Mans-winning DBR1 from the marque’s grand past will be parked in the dealerships as early as the first quarter of next year. The car will only be made in 88 limited edition units with each one costing a mind-bending $950,000 &#8211; so it’s going to be a rare affair to spot one the roads!</p>\n<p>The front of the Aston Martin V12 stamps the authority of road presence in every aspect, right from its headlights and the intimidating grille to the nostrils on the hood and well creased sporty design language flowing to the sides which features 21-inch forged center-locking wheels. The rear compliments those aesthetics very well with the spoiler that protrudes out of the taillights, demanding special attention. The car sports broadened shoulders and stylish twin humps and spine separating the driver and the co-rider. The Skyfall Silver livery designed in collaboration with Boeing is inspired by fighter jets and is aptly contrasted with the satin black on the exhaust tips, vent grilles, and vanes. To keep the total weight down without compromising the aesthetics, the design team has infused satin chrome structural carbon fiber and aluminum inserts.</p>\n<p>The heart of this machine is the 5.2-liter twin-turbocharged V-12 that churns out 710 horsepower and 555 pound-feet of torque. This sublime power translates to an impressive 0-62 mph in 3.5 seconds and a top speed of electronically limited 186 mph &#8211; if that doesn’t give you’re the adrenaline rush of driving on the open roads, we are afraid nothing will! Matt Becker, Aston Martin&#8217;s chief engineer, said, “For raw, driving thrills the V12 Speedster is unparalleled, the fully open element of the car adding a new dimension to the experience.” He believes that “driving doesn’t get any purer than this” thanks to the engaging driving experience with the power of twin-turbo 5.2-liter V12 at your command.</p>\n<p>Designer: <a href=\"https://www.astonmartin.com/en-us/models/future-models/v12-speedster#section_Overview\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Aston Martin</a></p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full 11:33:10","updatedTime":"2020-10-09 11:33:10","title":"Meet the smallest, slimmest 3-in-1 tripod stand to ever attach to your smartphone","link":"https://www.yankodesign.com/?p=280819","description":"<p><iframe title=\"LOOKSTAND: Most Functional Pocket-sized Phone/Tablet Stand\" src=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/lookstand/worlds-tallest-pocket-sized-phonestand/widget/video.html\" height=\"590.625\" width=\"1050\" frameborder=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\"></iframe></p>\n<p>The title of this article really doesn&#8217;t do justice to the LOOKSTAND, because it dilutes the LOOKSTAND to just four words &#8211; smallest, slimmest, tripod stand. In reality though, the LOOKSTAND is capable of more than just those things. Smaller than an Apple TV remote, the LOOKSTAND is a tripod, selfie-stick, and kickstand for your smartphone or tablet. It comes with an all-metal design that attaches to the back of your device (it&#8217;s removable too), giving you the freedom to interact with your phone either with your hands, or hands-free.</p>\n<p>The LOOKSTAND adheres to the back of your device using a slim plastic mount that sticks on with 3M adhesive. Designed to work universally with smartphones as well as with tablets, the LOOKSTAND weighs between 1.6 to 2.9 ounces (depending on the size variant you pick) and can easily support devices as heavy as 28 ounces. Its AL6061 Aluminum Alloy construction makes it robust yet deceptively light and thin, and the stand comes with a 360° hinge that lets you rotate and tilt your phone/tablet in landscape, portrait, or even in any intermediary angle. In the tripod mode, the LOOKSTAND can elevate your device to more than 7-inches off the ground using an adjustable telescopic system, turning your phone or tablet into an elevated hands-free device that&#8217;s ideal for whether you&#8217;re watching movies, attending a video call, using your device for work, or for making TikTok videos. Fold the tripod&#8217;s legs back into LOOKSTAND and it turns into a selfie stick that you can use to make dynamic videos or take group photos where everyone&#8217;s in the frame. A third mode allows you to use the LOOKSTAND as a regular kickstand, allowing it to prop your tablet or phone up like a standing photo-frame.</p>\n<p>The LOOKSTAND does the job of three separate products all integrated into one slim device. It comes in two sizes, the standard LOOKSTAND that&#8217;s perfect for smartphones, and a LOOKSTAND Max that works better with tablets, Nintendo Switches, and even projectors. At just 0.2-inches in thickness, the LOOKSTAND is thin enough to let you easily slide your phone into and out of your pocket. It detaches too, leaving behind just a slim plastic mount behind that&#8217;s barely tangible and supports your phone&#8217;s ability to be wirelessly charged.</p>\n<p>The LOOKSTAND&#8217;s evolved over the past two years, becoming even smaller, stronger, and better with time. Currently in its second edition, the stand quite literally helps uplift your phone/tablet experience. Whether you&#8217;re working from home, attending video calls, binge-watching Schitt&#8217;s Creek, exercising, or even creating content on your portable device, the LOOKSTAND has a unique ability to transform and cater to all those demands.</p>\n<p>Designer: Regina Koh</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/lookstand/worlds-tallest-pocket-sized-phonestand\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><strong>Click Here to Buy Now: $39</strong></a> <del datetime=\"2020-10-07T09:30:58+00:00\">$49</del> (20% off). It comes with an all-metal design that attaches to the back of your device (it&#8217;s removable too), giving you the freedom to interact with your phone either with your hands, or hands-free.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/lookstand/worlds-tallest-pocket-sized-phonestand\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"800\" /></a></p>\n<p>Both stands extend up to a height of a full 7-inches for the perfect, ergonomic viewing angle in both portrait and landscape modes to maximize sr-ugc.imgix.net/assets/030/887/449/302b6d03b74c9f9ee6c11988920498ce_original.gif?ixlib=rb-2.1.0&w=680&fit=max&v=1601970518&auto=format&gif-q=50&q=92&s=6a7d612b8a69c7cf74c1c020792bb44c":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn91@2020_2/2020/10/09/03-33-22-199_26f8660481767562.webp","https://ksr-ugc.imgix.net/assets/030/886/494/508952491009cb77fe6cd33466db9497_original.gif?ixlib=rb-2.1.0&w=680&fit=max&v=1601962613&auto=format&gif-q=50&q=92&s=3ee613f3038cfb86d9595ca30c156884":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn97@2020_6/2020/10/09/03-33-26-535_31f5f263a7cb87aa.webp","https://ksr-ugc.imgix.net/assets/030/886/678/9d8abed59c687830780c4158252d7c25_original.gif?ixlib=rb-2.1.0&w=680&fit=max&v=1601964475&auto=format&gif-q=50&q=92&s=877e2d545a46d9fb923b50a51a7f7504":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn94@2020_5/2020/10/09/03-33-25-397_0dbc47204f829764.webp","https://ksr-ugc.imgix.net/assets/030/886/872/6e0d5c99b069287338740d7fe440c20a_original.gif?ixlib=rb-2.1.0&w=680&fit=max&v=1601966168&auto=format&gif-q=50&q=92&s=400af13e3ee78c8d28a27d9512a3f472":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn84@2020_3/2020/10/09/03-33-21-737_4bfbc699187a1ef6.webp","https://ksr-ugc.imgix.net/assets/030/903/468/d88d8aceb694f7442eb194da2a81fd33_original.gif?ixlib=rb-2.1.0&w=680&fit=max&v=1602060133&auto=format&gif-q=50&q=92&s=dc8d8d2a453d7bdf99ce0e10916c89de":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn79@2020_4/2020/10/09/03-33-22-786_a71174969e813121.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/yankodesign?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn46@2020_6/2020/10/09/03-33-24-859_be70ddf18521ce99.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/yankodesign?i=jacl6T87WMI:roEp783SYAg:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn39@2020_5/2020/10/09/03-33-21-694_2f1756b2d746e738.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/yankodesign?d=7Q72WNTAKBA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn59@2020_6/2020/10/09/03-33-21-727_a7bab000502b2c11.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/yankodesign?i=jacl6T87WMI:roEp783SYAg:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn56@2020_4/2020/10/09/03-33-21-709_11b74fbe5f6c52c5.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/yankodesign?i=jacl6T87WMI:roEp783SYAg:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn20@2020_3/2020/10/09/03-33-21-734_0c182e4cdeb4b0dc.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/yankodesign?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn46@2020_5/2020/10/09/03-33-23-991_19238f9c81aa1a56.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/yankodesign/~4/jacl6T87WMI":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn72@2020_3/2020/10/09/03-33-21-635_308ba2254533fa03.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1602214390150},{"createdTime":"2020-10-09 11:33:10","updatedTime":"2020-10-09 11:33:10","title":"A 100% biodegradable adhesive-free shoe you can fully disassemble + compost in your backyard!","link":"https://www.yankodesign.com/?p=280590","description":"<p><iframe title=\"Forest Floor_Voronoi Runner\" width=\"1050\" height=\"591\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/dYVdoUNx_Qc?feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen></iframe></p>\n<p>At the back of our minds, we all want to make some difference to the deteriorating environment, and we do a thing or two consciously to prove a point. But one thing that we’ve all been doing otherwise – knowingly or unknowingly, there aren’t many options you’d argue – is using a pair of sneakers made from plastic or rubber. According to researchers, a pair of joggers you wear for the morning run takes upward of 30 years to decompose completely. While there is no clear definition of what makes a shoe sustainable, there are companies such as Adidas, Allbirds, and a few others, trying to build sneakers with recycled materials to address the issue &#8211; but it’s just not enough!</p>\n<p>Almost every pair of shoes currently being billed as sustainable uses some recycled or biodegradable materials. However, a strong adhesive is used to join these materials, which makes separating them difficult – leading to issues in end of life management. Designer Rik Olthuis from the Massey University of New Zealand has thought of a very innovative shoe design to overcome this lapse in eco-friendliness of footwear dubbed sustainable. The Voronoi Runners are made from 100-percent biodegradable materials, each of which can be separated easily at end of life to be composted. The result is a pair of sneakers you can wear and when done; you can separate each part of the shoe and send it down your backyard/kitchen compost to one day be used as manure for your garden – nothing remains behind, the Earth can breathe lighter and you can jog with your head held high.</p>\n<p>The main structure of Voronoi Runners is 3D printed using a robust, flexible biodegradable filament used to create the outsole and the midsole. The polyurethane foam is replaced by biodegradable alternative foam made using gelatine and glycerine, which offers comfy cushioning to the foot. Using 3D printing to create the midsole allows the Voronoi Runners to adapt to the individual wearer’s foot. The toe and heel caps printed from plant fibers add substance and shape to the Merino wool upper of the trainers that are also comfortable for everyday use. To eliminate the use of adhesive, the shoes are sewn using organic cotton thread and finished off with linen laces. This makes the Voronoi Runners easy to be dismantled fully and composted responsibly. Check out an on-foot video of the Voronoi below to get a hang of it.</p>\n<p>Designer: <a href=\"https://rikolthuis.design.blog/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Rik Olthuis</a></p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-280597\" 11:33:10","updatedTime":"2020-10-09 11:33:10","title":"This credit card sized wireless SSD lets you carry your own cloud server in your pocket!","link":"https://www.yankodesign.com/?p=281140","description":"<p><iframe title=\"skyBOX on Indiegogo\" width=\"1050\" height=\"591\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/ARbYJpJFRiQ?feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen></iframe></p>\n<p>The skyBOX is the second most powerful piece of tech you can fit into your pocket, after your smartphone. Designed to be the same dimension as a stack of credit cards, the skybox gives you the power of having your own Wi-Fi enabled cloud server in your pocket. It&#8217;s made to be universally compatible, working with any device that supports Wi-Fi connectivity, and comes with up to 4 terabytes of permanent storage. That&#8217;s enough to back up 50 smartphones, store millions of photos from your DSLR, or remotely host your own media server with over 5000 movies to choose from. Moreover, the skyBOX is wireless and portable, so you can carry it around in your pocket, accessing data no matter where you are.</p>\n<p>The most obvious benefit of having a wireless drive that&#8217;s with you anytime is that aside from its convenience, you don&#8217;t need to worry about paying hefty monthly subscription fees for cloud storage. The skyBOX comes with 4 storage tiers, ranging from 512GB to the whopping 4TB. Fitted with the latest generation in wifi technology &#8211; Wi-Fi 6, the skyBOX allows you to store files on it and retrieve data wirelessly at speeds as high as 900Mb/s. Whether it&#8217;s data from your smartphone, tablet, DSLR, or even work laptop, the skyBOX supports multiple device connectivity, giving you the freedom of sharing files between all your Wi-Fi enabled devices. In theory, that means you can edit videos shot from your camera directly on your smartphone or laptop without manually transferring files. You could, in theory, even watch those videos (or movies on your laptop) directly on your wifi-enabled TV.</p>\n<p>The skyBOX automatically enables data transfer between any devices within its wifi range, but a simple upgrade turns it into a remote cloud server too, essentially giving you the power to leave the skyBOX at home and access its files from anywhere, right through the skyBOX app. The app even lets you connect to your various cloud drives (Google, iCloud, OneDrive) and works seamlessly across Android, iOS, MacOS, and Windows platforms, giving you complete control over all your data and access to any file on any device.</p>\n<p>Designed to be universally compatible, wireless, and weigh just over 6 ounces, the skyBOX is perfect for photographers and videographers, allowing them to cross-share files between their DSLRs, drones, action cameras, and their phones, tablets, and laptops without worrying about cables, dongles, and ports. It&#8217;s also a great alternative to paying hundreds of dollars per year to Google, Apple, Microsoft, or Amazon to back up and store your device data. No matter what disk size you opt for (512GB, 1TB, 2TB, 4TB), you pay for it just once, and have complete ownership of and agency over your own data. Besides, I really like the idea of being able to practically carry your own server with you and use it to back your phone/tablet up while you store and watch hundreds of movies on any device for free!</p>\n<p>Designer: Superoc Design</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://skybox-credit-card-size.kckb.st/b4e1c977\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><strong>Click Here to Buy Now: $139</strong></a> <del datetime=\"2020-08-19T17:04:45+00:00\">$279</del> (50% off). 11:33:10","updatedTime":"2020-10-09 11:33:10","title":"This smart food storage device regulates temperature to keep your meals fresh in any climate!","link":"https://www.yankodesign.com/?p=280527","description":"<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-280519\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/10/mercedes-benz-new-electric-scooter-has-a-mileage-of-over-3100-miles-hello-zero-emissions/05-foodstorage_yankodesign.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p>I lived in various different climatic settings and one thing that is a persistent small problem causing large amounts of waste is storing food. If it is a tropical climate and you leave the food outside it will go bad due to the heat and if you are in somewhere cold and dry then you have to reheat your food in the microwave multiple times which is bad for your health. So how do we cover and store our food to reduce waste and effort? This conceptual device called The Mother&#8217;s Heart has the answers&#8230;yes, just like our mothers in the kitchen.</p>\n<p>There is a Korean practice of covering food with a cloth (Sang bo) which has been a tradition for centuries and has worked well &#8211; a ramie or silk fabric covering keeps it ventilated in the summers while a thicker fabric keeps it insulated in the winters. Inspired by this, the Mother&#8217;s Heart was designed to keep food fresh and retain its original nutrient quality. It is a simple device that is crafted like a dome food covering and an accompanying base plate. The covering has a dial on top and that lets you adjust the settings based on the food you&#8217;ve cooked. You can select between refrigeration or warmth and there is a timer feature that lets you select for how long you want to keep it running. The bottom heating coil can maintain an internal temperature of 60 Celcius or higher to store food like noodles and curry. The upper cooling fan can keep the temperature below 5 Celcius to store dishes like salads or sandwiches.</p>\n<p>&#8220;When I came home and lift up the cloth to have my meal, I could feel my mother&#8217;s warmth in the warmth of the rice. This design is inspired by sang bo so that mothers can still give their children fresh meals infused with their love,&#8221; elaborates Seojoung as he recalls the nostalgia that led him to create the award-winning Mother&#8217;s Heart. This is not only a convenient device for mothers but also anyone who works and cooks their own meals. It has the ability to help us reduce food waste and consume radiation-free meals. While meal-prep is great, there is nothing like a freshly cooked meal after you finish your chores &#8211; no one likes a wilted lettuce salad or a microwaved mac-n-cheese.</p>\n<p>Designer: Yu Seojoung</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-280515\" 11:33:10","updatedTime":"2020-10-09 11:33:10","title":"Starbucks redesigns their pour-over stand to amplify coffee lovers experience of brewing their coffee!","link":"https://www.yankodesign.com/?p=280834","description":"<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-280844\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/10/280834/7_Ivy-Pourover_Tai-Geng_Starbucks-Reserve-coffee-filter.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<p class=\"p1\">A Starbucks Reserve roastery, unlike its standard locations, is more than a pitstop on work commute or a place to write this article (in a pre-pandemic world). It looks like a high-end bar or brewery, with comfy couches and long, empty wooden counters. A Starbucks Reserve is not just a cafe: it’s an experience, one that invites the drinker to observe and appreciate the coffee-making process.</p>\n<p class=\"p1\">The first thing that hits us, even before entering a Starbucks store, is that intoxicating smell of coffee which acts as a siren to all the caffeine addicts. It is this anticipation and vibe that Starbucks captures, not just with its setting, but with its espresso-making tools, like the IVY Pour-Over coffee maker. Its clean, elegant design fits its environment perfectly. The holder is the same shade as the Starbucks paper cup and complements the brand’s overall color scheme. Also, unlike bulky metal espresso makers that block your hardworking baristas from view, the IVY lets you watch the coffee drip down into the cup. The Starbucks Reserve also fosters this behind-the-scenes brewing experience with its minimalistic <a href=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/2020/06/18/starbucks-redesigns-their-espresso-machines-to-use-gravity-for-a-smoother-coffee/?fbclid=IwAR1owu0Bb-DMqsqj_Mqyhwfbw6HELzfq6_ZVGyZ60lVZUrWeXCH1nmNbUr8\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Phantom Espresso maker</a>, which Yanko Design previously covered. The IVY Pour-Over was designed to brew a top-notch cup of coffee. The metal cone helps distribute heat evenly, which ensures that each brew is consistently high-quality. The grooves inside allow for optimal airflow between the paper filter and the cone’s walls, allowing the coffee to bloom and release more flavor. There&#8217;s even a small lip on the funnel that helps create the perfect stream of coffee, avoiding any rough splashes or drips.</p>\n<p class=\"p1\">The best part about the IVY Pour-Over is that you can take it home with you. It&#8217;s available for purchase at Starbucks Reserve locations and, more importantly, is designed to adapt to your coffee-drinking routine. You can display the stand proudly on your kitchen counter or, if you prefer a more mobile coffee-filter, detach the metal cone and place it on your mug. Simple. The IVY doesn&#8217;t fully capture the ambiance of a Starbucks Reserve, but it is a worthy substitute to satisfy homebound coffee fans.</p>\n<p>Designer: Tai Geng</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-280838\" src=\"https://www.yankodesign.com/images/design_news/2020/10/280834/1_Ivy-Pourover_Tai-Geng_Starbucks-Reserve-coffee-filter.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1050\" height=\"700\"
